                                    6789              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6790              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6791              Ÿ  COMMAND - main command loop                                        Ÿ
                                    6792              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6793              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6794              Ÿ  This routine is called at the completion of each command.          Ÿ
                                    6795              Ÿ  The routine cleans up after the previous command, and              Ÿ
                                    6796              Ÿ  re-initializes local cells, and then branches to get the           Ÿ
                                    6797              Ÿ  the next command.                                                  Ÿ
                                    6798              Ÿ        (The next command is then scanned, the scanner               Ÿ
                                    6799              Ÿ  branching to the correct routine to execute the given              Ÿ
                                    6800              Ÿ  command.  Upon command completion the command returns              Ÿ
                                    6801              Ÿ  here. And on and on !)                                             Ÿ
                                    6802              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6803              Ÿ  NOTE: the cleanup routine has no particular logic, except          Ÿ
                                    6804              Ÿ  to do the things that are required at command termination          Ÿ
                                    6805              Ÿ  It handles normal and abnormal terminations.  It is a hodge-       Ÿ
                                    6806              Ÿ  podge of stuff, some order dependent, some not.  It not            Ÿ
                                    6807              Ÿ  a pretty sight, but there are worse routines.                      Ÿ
                                    6808              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6809              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                    6810              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ

                                   10758              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   10759              Ÿ  STKCHK -- Routine to check that we haven't overflowed the          Ÿ
                                   10760              Ÿ    stack.  Note that usually the stack check in the dispatcher      Ÿ
                                   10761              Ÿ    catches stack overflows.  Routines that are sensitive to         Ÿ
                                   10762              Ÿ    stack overflows will call this routine to make sure that         Ÿ

                                   24495              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   24496              Ÿ  CHECKTRY - Check if command to TRY is special/invalid              Ÿ
                                   24497              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                   24498              Ÿ  Special TRY sets CPFXXTRY,  this flag remains set till next        Ÿ
                                   24499              Ÿ  exec command from an exec file is executed.  That is the           Ÿ
                                   24500              Ÿ  CPFXXTRY flag survives a EDTCOM call, CPFTRY does not.  This       Ÿ
                                   24501              Ÿ  allows VIEW (which executes other commands in PAGE mode) to        Ÿ
                                   24502              Ÿ  not break if CPFXXTRY is set.  On the other hand, a TRY READ       Ÿ
                                   24503              Ÿ  that executes a bad command, may cause a break. Which is           Ÿ
                                   24504              Ÿ  presumably what we want.  GET and PUT are special cases.           Ÿ
                                   24505              Ÿ  They are the only ORVYL commands that can be TRYed. This is        Ÿ
                                   24506              Ÿ  tricky code.  All so we can use TRY for GET, PUT, and VIEW.        Ÿ
                                   24507              Ÿ  And View may not even work. YUK !                                  Ÿ
                                   24508              Ÿ                                                                     Ÿ
                                                      ¾þþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþþ»
